			<h2>A Globally Recognized Avatar</h2>

			<p class="intro">Your Gravatar is an image that follows you from site to site appearing beside your name when you do things like comment or post on a blog. Avatars help identify your posts on blogs and web forums, so why not on any&nbsp;site?</p>

userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><p>Today Mark shared a letter about giving people the power to build a global community. For the past decade, Facebook has focused on connecting friends and families. With that foundation, our next focus will be developing the social infrastructure for community -- for supporting us, for keeping us safe, for informing us, for civic engagement, and for inclusion of all. Please check it out and let us know what you think!</p></div><div class="_3x-2"><div data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;H&quot;&#125;"></div><div><div class="_5r69"><div class="clearfix mtm"><a class="lfloat _ohe" href="/notes/mark-zuckerberg/building-global-community/10103508221158471/"><img class="_s0 _54ru img" src="https://scontent.fbsb9-1.fna.fbcdn.net/v/t34.0-1/p32x32/16176889_112685309244626_578204711_n.jpg?oh=717c3e769f497c266981eff5a25d0791&amp;oe=58DD71EA" alt="" /></a><div class="plm _42ef"><span class="mbs _11dd fwn fcg" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;C&quot;&#125;"><span class="fwb" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;;&quot;&#125;"><a href="https://www.facebook.com/zuck?hc_ref=PAGES_TIMELINE&amp;fref=nf">Mark Zuckerberg</a></span></span><div class="_5pcp _5lel"><span class="_5paw _14zs" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;j&quot;&#125;"><a class="_3e_2 _14zr" href="#"></a></span><span role="presentation" aria-hidden="true"> · </span><span><span class="fsm fwn fcg"><a class="_5pcq" href="/notes/mark-zuckerberg/building-global-community/10103508221158471/" target=""><abbr title="Thursday, February 16, 2017 at 12:56pm" data-utime="1487278594" data-shorten="1" class="_5ptz"><span class="timestampContent">February 16</span></abbr></a></span></span><span role="presentation" aria-hidden="true"> · </span><a data-hover="tooltip" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator _5pcq" aria-label="Shared with: Public" href="#" role="button" id="u_0_m"><i class="lock img sp_euCDsy2vhU4 sx_0a0ec1"></i></a></div><div class="mtm _5pco" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><p>I know a lot of us are thinking about how we can make the most positive impact in the world right now.     (function (window, document) {
      var regexApp = function () {
        return /MobApp_Android|MobApp_iOS|MobApp_WP/;
      };

      var getUserAgent = function () {
        if (window.getUserAgent) {
          return window.getUserAgent();
        }
        return window.navigator.userAgent;
      };

      var extractAppFromUserAgent = function () {
        var appUserAgent, appVars, index, ua, userAgentParts;
        ua = getUserAgent();
        userAgentParts = ua.split(' ');
        for (index in userAgentParts) {
          appUserAgent = userAgentParts[index];
          if (regexApp().test(appUserAgent)) {
            appVars = appUserAgent.split('/');
            return {
              name: appVars[0].replace('_', ' '),
              version: appVars[1],
              frameworkVersion: appVars[2]
            };
          }
        }
        return null;
      };

      var addGlbOnAppClass = function () {
        var frameworkVersion, nativeAppInfo;
        nativeAppInfo = extractAppFromUserAgent();
        if (nativeAppInfo !== null) {
          if (nativeAppInfo.frameworkVersion) {
            frameworkVersion = parseInt(nativeAppInfo.frameworkVersion, 10);
            if (frameworkVersion >= 1) {
              document.documentElement.className += ' glb-on-app';
            }
          }
        }
      };

      addGlbOnAppClass(); // Garante que o header irá sumir rápido
    })(window, document);

rel="nordeste/ba/salvador" /></map><div class="informacoes"><p class="titulo">tempo no <span>Brasil</span></p><p class="descricao">Sistema de baixa pressão na costa do ES forma muita instabilidade sobre o Estado nesta terça-feira. Este sistema provoca chuva que pode ser forte também no centro-norte de MG. Nas áreas próximas do litoral entre SC e o RJ, por causa dos ventos úmidos marítimos, há possibilidade para chuva fraca ao longo do período. No interior do Sul e de SP, além das áreas do sul de MG, o sol predomina e não chove. O dia começa com temperatura amena. No Nordeste, risco para chuva forte entre o CE e o MA. No Norte, chuva em toda a Região. </p><a href="#" title="mais">mais</a></div></div><div class="menu"><ul><li><a href="#" class="titulo norte" title="Norte" rel="norte"><strong>Norte</strong></a><ul><li class="manaus"><a href="/previsao-do-tempo/am/manaus.html" title="Manaus (AM)" rel="norte/am/manaus">Manaus -
